### **Me** - 2025-12-22 16:44:09

Foundation of understanding:
- it is impossible to know if god exists (finite cannot comprehend the infinite)
- nearly everything is uncertain (finite beings understand in part)
- all knowledge is a conjecture (an opinion or conclusion formed on the basis of incomplete information)
- we come up with our best bold conjectures and falsification is how we make progress in understanding

From this, I believe:
- agnosticism (the belief that nothing is known or can be known of the existence or nature of God)
- sure existence is eternal
- all things are natural
- life is growth and motion
- we should promote life
- we should end disease and death
- we should seek peace, fun, awe, and novelty
- ethics and morality are man made and are how we all get along
